@resolution_weight_hated = 3
@resolution_weight_disliked = 4
@resolution_weight_unpopular = 5
@resolution_weight_normal = 6
@resolution_weight_popular = 6.5
@resolution_weight_liked = 6.5
@resolution_weight_loved = 7

@resolution_cost_t1 = 100
@resolution_cost_t2 = 150
@resolution_cost_t3 = 200
@resolution_cost_t4 = 250
@resolution_cost_t5 = 300
@resolution_cost_t6 = 500
@resolution_cost_denounce = 25

@resolution_flag_timer = 360

# Custom Resolutions !

resolution_discovery_archeology_repeal_1 = {
	icon = "GFX_repeal_blue"

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t1
		}
	}
	target = no

	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = resolution_discovery_archeology_repeal_1_effect_success
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed_discovery_archeology_repeal days = @resolution_flag_timer }
		}
	}

	fail_effects = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_failed_discovery_archeology_repeal days = @resolution_flag_timer }
		}
	}

	potential = {
		is_active_resolution = "resolution_discovery_archeology_1"
	}

	allow = {}

	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_unpopular

		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_materialist = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1
			is_xenophobe = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			is_spiritualist = yes
		}
			}
}

resolution_discovery_archeology_1 = {
	icon = "GFX_resolution_discovery_archeology"

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t1
		}
	}
	
	target = no
	level = 1

	modifier = {
		resolution_discovery_archeology_1 = 1
	}

	effect = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_global_flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed_discovery_archeology days = @resolution_flag_timer }
		}
	}

	fail_effects = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_failed_discovery_archeology days = @resolution_flag_timer }
		}
	}

	allow = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			fail_text = "resolution_already_active"
			NOR = {
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_discovery_archeology_1"
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_discovery_archeology_2"
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_discovery_archeology_3"
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_discovery_archeology_4"
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_discovery_archeology_5"
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_discovery_archeology_6"
			}
		}
	}

	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_loved

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			is_materialist = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			is_xenophile = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_xenophobe = yes
		}
	}
}

resolution_ecology_repeal_6 = {
	icon = "GFX_repeal_blue"

	potential = {
		has_federations_dlc = yes
	}

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t6
		}
	}
	target = no

	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = resolution_ecology_repeal_6_effect_success
		hidden_effect = {
			pass_resolution = "resolution_ecology_paradise_initiative"
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed_ecology_repeal days = @resolution_flag_timer }
		}
		custom_tooltip = resolution_ecology_paradise_initiative_tooltip
	}

	fail_effects = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_failed_ecology_repeal days = @resolution_flag_timer }
		}
	}

	potential = {
		is_active_resolution = "resolution_ecology_6"
	}


	modifier = {
		resolution_ecology_recycling_initiatives = 1
		resolution_ecology_natural_sanctuaries = 1
		resolution_ecology_integrated_gardens = 1
		resolution_ecology_environmental_control_board = 1
		resolution_ecology_paradise_initative = 1
	}

	allow = {}

	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_unpopular

		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			has_valid_civic = civic_environmentalist
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			has_valid_civic = civic_agrarian_idyll
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			OR = {
				has_valid_civic = civic_mining_guilds
				has_valid_civic = civic_machine_rockbreakers
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			country_uses_food = no
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			is_lithoid_empire = yes
		}
	}
}

	icon = "GFX_resolution_galactic_studies"

	potential = {
		has_federations_dlc = yes
	}

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t6
		}
	}
	target = no

		resolution_galacticstudies_cooperative_research_channels = 1
		resolution_galacticstudies_astral_studies_network = 1
		resolution_galacticstudies_advanced_xenostudies = 1
		resolution_galacticstudies_ethical_guideline_refactoring = 1
		resolution_galacticstudies_extradimensional_experimentation = 1
		resolution_galacticstudies_6 = 1
	}

	effect = {
		
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed_galacticstudies days = @resolution_flag_timer }

			every_playable_country = {
				limit = { is_galactic_community_member = yes }
				country_event = { id = federations.10020 days = 3 }
			}
		}
	}

	fail_effects = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_failed_galacticstudies days = @resolution_flag_timer }
		}
	}

	allow = {
		is_active_resolution = "resolution_galacticstudies_extradimensional_experimentation"
	}

	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_disliked

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			is_materialist = yes
		}
	}
}

resolution_greatergood_6 = {
	icon = "GFX_resolution_greater_good"

	potential = {
		has_federations_dlc = yes
	}

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t6
		}
	}
	target = no

	modifier = {
		resolution_greatergood_workers_rights = 1
		resolution_greatergood_five_year_plans = 1
		resolution_greatergood_greater_than_ourselves = 1
		resolution_greatergood_balance_in_the_middle = 1
		resolution_greatergood_universal_prosperity_mandate = 1
		resolution_greatergood_6 = 1
	}

	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = resolution_greatergood_universal_prosperity_mandate_tooltip
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed_greatergood days = @resolution_flag_timer }
		}
	}

	fail_effects = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_failed_greatergood days = @resolution_flag_timer }
		}
	}

	allow = {
		is_active_resolution = "resolution_greatergood_universal_prosperity_mandate"
	}

	breach = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				is_gestalt = no
				any_owned_species = {
					is_sapient = yes
					OR = {
						has_living_standard = { type = living_standard_subsistence country = prev}
						has_living_standard = { type = living_standard_stratified country = prev}
						has_living_standard = { type = living_standard_normal country = prev}
						has_living_standard = { type = living_standard_academic_privilege country = prev}
						has_living_standard = { type = living_standard_good country = prev}
					}
				}
			}
			AND = {
				is_gestalt = yes
				any_owned_species = {
					is_sapient = yes
					has_living_standard = { type = living_standard_ego_assimilation }
				}
			}
		}

	}

	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_disliked

		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_egalitarian = no
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_megacorp = yes
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			is_egalitarian = yes
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_egalitarian
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			OR = {
				has_valid_civic = civic_shared_burden
				has_valid_civic = civic_machine_servitor
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			OR = {
				has_valid_civic = civic_agrarian_idyll
				has_valid_civic = civic_free_haven
				has_valid_civic = civic_idealistic_foundation
				has_valid_civic = civic_inwards_perfection
			}
		}
	}
}

# Custom Sanctions !

resolution_sanctions_tech_repeal_4 = {
	icon = "GFX_repeal_blue"

	potential = {
		has_federations_dlc = yes
	}

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_denounce
		}
	}
	target = no

	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = resolution_sanctions_tech_repeal_4_effect_success
		hidden_effect = {
			pass_resolution = "resolution_sanctions_tech_3"
		}
	}

	potential = {
		is_active_resolution = "resolution_sanctions_tech_4"
	}

	triggered_modifier = {
		potential = {
			OR = {
				is_in_breach_of_any = yes
				has_modifier = resolution_denounced
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			resolution_sanctions_tech = 3
		}
	}

	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_unpopular

		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_in_breach_of_any = yes
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			is_in_breach_of_any = no
			is_materialist = yes
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			any_relation = {
				is_in_federation_with = prev

				OR = {
					is_in_breach_of_any = yes
					has_modifier = resolution_denounced
				}
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			any_relation = {
				is_rival = prev

				OR = {
					is_in_breach_of_any = yes
					has_modifier = resolution_denounced
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			any_relation = {
				is_in_federation_with = prev

				OR = {
					is_in_breach_of_any = yes
					has_modifier = resolution_denounced
				}
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			any_relation = {
				is_rival = prev

				OR = {
					is_in_breach_of_any = yes
					has_modifier = resolution_denounced
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

## Vanilla Resolutions

# Galactic Market Resolutions
resolution_galactic_market_form = {
	icon = "GFX_resolution_form_galactic_market"

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t1
		}
	}
	target = no

	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = resolution_galactic_market_form_effect_success
		hidden_effect = {
			# Kickoff the Forming the Market event chain
			country_event = { id = action.96 }

			set_global_flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed

			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed_general days = @resolution_flag_timer }
		}
	}

	fail_effects = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_failed_general days = @resolution_flag_timer }
		}
	}

	modifier = {
		country_resource_max_add = 10000
	}

	potential = {
		NOR = {
			has_global_flag = galactic_market_founded
			has_global_flag = ongoing_market_nomination
		}

		is_gestalt = no
		is_homicidal = no
		count_diplo_ties = {
			limit = {
				is_country_type = default
				is_homicidal = no
			}
			count >= 3
		}
	}

	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_popular

		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			has_authority = auth_corporate
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			OR = {
				has_ai_personality = peaceful_traders
				has_ai_personality = ruthless_capitalists
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			has_ai_personality = xenophobic_isolationists
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			is_xenophobe = yes
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			years_passed > 50
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			years_passed > 100
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			years_passed > 150
		}
	}
}

	}

		}
	}

		}

	icon = "GFX_resolution_ecolgical_protection"

	potential = {
		has_federations_dlc = yes
	}

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t4
		}
	}
	target = no
	level = 4

	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = resolution_ecology_environmental_control_board_tooltip
		hidden_effect = {
			set_global_flag = resolution_with_breach_effect_passed
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed_ecology days = @resolution_flag_timer }
		}
	}

	fail_effects = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_failed_ecology days = @resolution_flag_timer }
		}
	}

	modifier = {
		resolution_ecology_recycling_initiatives = 1
		resolution_ecology_natural_sanctuaries = 1
		resolution_ecology_integrated_gardens = 1
		resolution_ecology_environmental_control_board = 1
	}

	allow = {
		is_active_resolution = "resolution_ecology_integrated_gardens"
	}

	breach = {
		has_country_flag = resolution_breached_terraformed
	}

	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_unpopular

		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			in_breach_of = resolution_ecology_environmental_control_board
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			has_valid_civic = civic_environmentalist
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			has_valid_civic = civic_agrarian_idyll
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			OR = {
				has_valid_civic = civic_mining_guilds
				has_valid_civic = civic_machine_rockbreakers
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			country_uses_food = no
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_lithoid_empire = yes
		}
	}
}

resolution_galacticstudies_advanced_xenostudies = {
	icon = "GFX_resolution_galactic_studies"

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t3
		}
	}
	target = no
	level = 3

	modifier = {
		resolution_galacticstudies_cooperative_research_channels = 1
		resolution_galacticstudies_astral_studies_network = 1
		resolution_galacticstudies_advanced_xenostudies = 1
	}

	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = resolution_galacticstudies_advanced_xenostudies_tooltip
		hidden_effect = {
			set_global_flag = resolution_with_breach_effect_passed
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed_galacticstudies days = @resolution_flag_timer }
			every_playable_country = {
				limit = {
					is_galactic_community_member = yes
					OR = {
						AND = {
							can_set_ai_policy = yes
							has_policy_flag = ai_outlawed
						}

						AND = {
							has_met_primitives = yes
							has_policy_flag = interference_passive
						}
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = federations.10100 }
			}
		}
	}

	fail_effects = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_failed_galacticstudies days = @resolution_flag_timer }
		}
	}

	allow = {
		is_active_resolution = "resolution_galacticstudies_astral_studies_network"
	}

	breach = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				can_set_ai_policy = yes
				has_policy_flag = ai_outlawed
			}

			AND = {
				has_met_primitives = yes
				has_policy_flag = interference_passive
			}
		}
	}

	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_normal

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			is_materialist = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			is_spiritualist = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_xenophile = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			in_breach_of = resolution_galacticstudies_advanced_xenostudies
		}
	}
}

	icon = "GFX_resolution_galactic_studies"

	potential = {
		has_federations_dlc = yes
	}

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t4
		}
	}
	target = no
	level = 4

	modifier = {
		resolution_galacticstudies_cooperative_research_channels = 1
		resolution_galacticstudies_astral_studies_network = 1
		resolution_galacticstudies_advanced_xenostudies = 1
		resolution_galacticstudies_ethical_guideline_refactoring = 1
	}

	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = resolution_galacticstudies_ethical_guideline_refactoring_tooltip
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed_galacticstudies days = @resolution_flag_timer }

			every_playable_country = {
				limit = {
					is_galactic_community_member = yes
					OR = {
						AND = {
							has_technology = tech_selected_lineages
							has_policy_flag = leader_enhancement_natural_selection
						}

						AND = {
							has_technology = tech_capacity_boosters
							NOT = { has_policy_flag = leader_enhancement_capacity_boosters }
						}
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = federations.10110 }
			}
		}
	}

	fail_effects = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_failed_galacticstudies days = @resolution_flag_timer }
		}
	}

	allow = {
		is_active_resolution = "resolution_galacticstudies_advanced_xenostudies"
	}

	breach = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				has_technology = tech_selected_lineages
				has_policy_flag = leader_enhancement_natural_selection
			}

			AND = {
				has_technology = tech_capacity_boosters
				NOT = { has_policy_flag = leader_enhancement_capacity_boosters }
			}
		}
	}

	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_unpopular

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			is_materialist = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75

		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_egalitarian = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			in_breach_of = resolution_galacticstudies_ethical_guideline_refactoring
		}
	}
}

		}

		}
	}

			OR = {

				has_valid_civic = civic_trading_posts

resolution_greatergood_repeal_1 = {
	icon = "GFX_resolution_council_veto"

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t1
		}
	}
	target = no

	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = resolution_greatergood_repeal_1_effect_success
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed_greatergood_repeal days = @resolution_flag_timer }
		}
	}

	fail_effects = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_failed_greatergood_repeal days = @resolution_flag_timer }
		}
	}

	potential = {
		is_active_resolution = "resolution_greatergood_workers_rights"
	}

	allow = {}

	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_unpopular

		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_egalitarian = yes
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			is_authoritarian = yes
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			OR = {
				has_valid_civic = civic_agrarian_idyll
				has_valid_civic = civic_free_haven
				has_valid_civic = civic_idealistic_foundation
				has_valid_civic = civic_inwards_perfection
				has_valid_civic = civic_machine_servitor
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			OR = {
				has_valid_civic = civic_slaver_guilds
				has_valid_civic = civic_indentured_assets
				is_slaver = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

resolution_greatergood_workers_rights = {
	icon = "GFX_resolution_greater_good"

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t1
		}
	}
	target = no
	level = 1

	modifier = {
		resolution_greatergood_workers_rights = 1
	}

	effect = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_global_flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed_greatergood days = @resolution_flag_timer }
		}
	}

	fail_effects = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_failed_greatergood days = @resolution_flag_timer }
		}
	}

	allow = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			fail_text = "resolution_already_active"
			NOR = {
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_greatergood_workers_rights"
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_greatergood_five_year_plans"
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_greatergood_greater_than_ourselves"
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_greatergood_balance_in_the_middle"
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_greatergood_universal_prosperity_mandate"
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_greatergood_6"
			}
		}
	}

	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_loved

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			is_egalitarian = yes
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			is_authoritarian = yes
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_megacorp = yes
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_egalitarian
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			OR = {
				has_valid_civic = civic_shared_burden
				has_valid_civic = civic_machine_servitor
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			OR = {
				has_valid_civic = civic_agrarian_idyll
				has_valid_civic = civic_free_haven
				has_valid_civic = civic_idealistic_foundation
				has_valid_civic = civic_inwards_perfection
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			OR = {
				is_gestalt = yes
				has_valid_civic = civic_aristocratic_elite
				has_valid_civic = civic_police_state
			}

		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			OR = {
				has_valid_civic = civic_slaver_guilds
				has_valid_civic = civic_indentured_assets
				is_slaver = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

resolution_greatergood_five_year_plans = {
	icon = "GFX_resolution_greater_good"

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t2
		}
	}
	target = no
	level = 2

	modifier = {
		resolution_greatergood_workers_rights = 1
		resolution_greatergood_five_year_plans = 1
	}

	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = resolution_greatergood_five_year_plans_tooltip
		hidden_effect = {
			set_global_flag = resolution_with_breach_effect_passed
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed_greatergood days = @resolution_flag_timer }
			every_playable_country = {
				limit = {
					is_galactic_community_member = yes
					is_gestalt = no
					any_owned_species = {
						is_sapient = yes
						has_living_standard = { type = living_standard_subsistence country = prev }
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = federations.10200 }
			}
		}
	}

	fail_effects = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_failed_greatergood days = @resolution_flag_timer }
		}
	}

	allow = {
		is_active_resolution = "resolution_greatergood_workers_rights"
	}

	breach = {
		is_gestalt = no
		any_owned_species = {
			is_sapient = yes
			has_living_standard = { type = living_standard_subsistence country = prev }
		}
	}

	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_popular

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			is_egalitarian = yes
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			is_authoritarian = yes
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			in_breach_of = resolution_greatergood_five_year_plans
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_megacorp = yes
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_egalitarian
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			OR = {
				has_valid_civic = civic_shared_burden
				has_valid_civic = civic_machine_servitor
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.6
			is_authoritarian = yes
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			OR = {
				has_valid_civic = civic_slaver_guilds
				has_valid_civic = civic_indentured_assets
				is_slaver = yes
				any_owned_species = {
					is_sapient = yes
					has_living_standard = { type = living_standard_subsistence country = prev }
				}
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			OR = {
				has_valid_civic = civic_agrarian_idyll
				has_valid_civic = civic_free_haven
				has_valid_civic = civic_idealistic_foundation
				has_valid_civic = civic_inwards_perfection
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			OR = {
				is_gestalt = yes
				has_valid_civic = civic_aristocratic_elite
				has_valid_civic = civic_police_state
			}
		}
	}

resolution_greatergood_greater_than_ourselves = {
	icon = "GFX_resolution_greater_good"

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t3
		}
	}
	target = no
	level = 3

	modifier = {
		resolution_greatergood_workers_rights = 1
		resolution_greatergood_five_year_plans = 1
		resolution_greatergood_greater_than_ourselves = 1
	}

	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = resolution_greatergood_greater_than_ourselves_tooltip

		hidden_effect = {
			every_playable_country = {
				limit = { is_galactic_community_member = yes }
				country_event = { id = federations.10010 days = 15 }
			}

			every_playable_country = {
				limit = {
					is_galactic_community_member = yes

					OR = {
						any_enslaved_species = {
							is_sapient = yes
							OR = {
								has_slavery_type = { type = slavery_normal country = prev  }
								has_slavery_type = { type = slavery_livestock country = prev }
								has_slavery_type = { type = slavery_matrix country = prev }
							}
						}
						AND = {
							is_gestalt = no
							any_owned_species = {
								is_sapient = yes
								OR = {
									has_living_standard = { type = living_standard_subsistence country = prev }
									has_living_standard = { type = living_standard_stratified country = prev }
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = federations.10210 }
			}

			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed_greatergood days = @resolution_flag_timer }
		}
	}

	fail_effects = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_failed_greatergood days = @resolution_flag_timer }
		}
	}

	allow = {
		is_active_resolution = "resolution_greatergood_five_year_plans"
	}

	breach = {
		OR = {
			any_enslaved_species = {
				is_sapient = yes
				OR = {
					has_slavery_type = { type = slavery_normal country = prev }
					has_slavery_type = { type = slavery_livestock country = prev }
					has_slavery_type = { type = slavery_matrix country = prev }
				}
			}
			AND = {
				is_gestalt = no
				any_owned_species = {
					is_sapient = yes
					OR = {
						has_living_standard = { type = living_standard_subsistence country = prev }
						has_living_standard = { type = living_standard_stratified country = prev }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_normal

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			is_egalitarian = yes
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			is_authoritarian = yes
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			in_breach_of = resolution_greatergood_greater_than_ourselves
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_megacorp = yes
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_egalitarian
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			OR = {
				has_valid_civic = civic_shared_burden
				has_valid_civic = civic_machine_servitor
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.6
			OR = {
				is_authoritarian = yes
				is_gestalt = yes
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			OR = {
				has_valid_civic = civic_slaver_guilds
				has_valid_civic = civic_indentured_assets
				is_slaver = yes
				any_owned_species = {
					is_sapient = yes
					OR = {
						has_living_standard = { type = living_standard_subsistence country = prev }
						has_living_standard = { type = living_standard_stratified country = prev }
					}
				}
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			OR = {
				has_valid_civic = civic_agrarian_idyll
				has_valid_civic = civic_free_haven
				has_valid_civic = civic_idealistic_foundation
				has_valid_civic = civic_inwards_perfection
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			OR = {
				has_valid_civic = civic_aristocratic_elite
				has_valid_civic = civic_police_state
			}
		}
	}
}

resolution_greatergood_balance_in_the_middle = {
	icon = "GFX_resolution_greater_good"

	potential = {
		has_federations_dlc = yes
	}

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t4
		}
	}
	target = no
	level = 4

	modifier = {
		resolution_greatergood_workers_rights = 1
		resolution_greatergood_five_year_plans = 1
		resolution_greatergood_greater_than_ourselves = 1
		resolution_greatergood_balance_in_the_middle = 1
	}

	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = resolution_greatergood_balance_in_the_middle_tooltip
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed_greatergood days = @resolution_flag_timer }

			every_playable_country = {
				limit = {
					is_galactic_community_member = yes

					OR = {
						any_owned_species = {
							is_sapient = yes
							has_citizenship_type = { type = citizenship_slavery country = prev }
						}
						AND = {
							is_gestalt = no
							any_owned_species = {
								is_sapient = yes
								OR = {
									has_living_standard = { type = living_standard_subsistence country = prev }
									has_living_standard = { type = living_standard_stratified country = prev }
									has_living_standard = { type = living_standard_normal country = prev }
									has_living_standard = { type = living_standard_academic_privilege country = prev }
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = federations.10220 }
			}
		}
	}

	fail_effects = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_failed_greatergood days = @resolution_flag_timer }
		}
	}

	allow = {
		is_active_resolution = "resolution_greatergood_greater_than_ourselves"
	}

	breach = {
		OR = {
			has_valid_civic = civic_indentured_assets
			has_valid_civic = civic_slaver_guilds
			any_owned_species = {
				is_sapient = yes
				has_citizenship_type = { type = citizenship_slavery country = prev }
			}
			AND = {
				is_gestalt = no
				any_owned_species = {
					is_sapient = yes
					OR = {
						has_living_standard = { type = living_standard_subsistence country = prev }
						has_living_standard = { type = living_standard_stratified country = prev }
						has_living_standard = { type = living_standard_normal country = prev }
						has_living_standard = { type = living_standard_academic_privilege country = prev }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_unpopular

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			is_egalitarian = yes
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			is_authoritarian = yes
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			in_breach_of = resolution_greatergood_balance_in_the_middle
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_megacorp = yes
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_egalitarian
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			OR = {
				has_valid_civic = civic_shared_burden
				has_valid_civic = civic_machine_servitor
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.6
			OR = {
				is_authoritarian = yes
				is_gestalt = yes
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			OR = {
				has_valid_civic = civic_slaver_guilds
				has_valid_civic = civic_indentured_assets
				is_slaver = yes
				any_owned_species = {
					is_sapient = yes
					OR = {
						has_living_standard = { type = living_standard_subsistence country = prev }
						has_living_standard = { type = living_standard_stratified country = prev }
						has_living_standard = { type = living_standard_normal country = prev }
						has_living_standard = { type = living_standard_academic_privilege country = prev }
					}
				}
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			OR = {
				has_valid_civic = civic_agrarian_idyll
				has_valid_civic = civic_free_haven
				has_valid_civic = civic_idealistic_foundation
				has_valid_civic = civic_inwards_perfection
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			OR = {
				has_valid_civic = civic_aristocratic_elite
				has_valid_civic = civic_police_state
			}
		}
	}
}

				has_valid_civic = civic_warrior_culture
				has_valid_civic = civic_private_military_companies

resolution_mutualdefense_castigation_denouncement = {
	icon = "GFX_resolution_mutual_defense"

	potential = {
		has_federations_dlc = yes
	}

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_denounce
		}
	}

	target = yes
	harmful = yes
	valid_target = {
		is_country_type = default
		NOT = { is_same_value = from } # don't denounce yourself.
		OR = {
			is_galactic_community_member = no
			is_in_breach_of_any = yes
		}
		OR = {
			opinion_level = { who = from level < neutral }
			from = { is_rival = prev }
			is_in_breach_of_any = yes
		}
	}

	effect = {
		add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_denounced days = 3600 }
	}

	potential = {
		OR = {
			is_active_resolution = "resolution_mutualdefense_castigation_proclamation"
			is_active_resolution = "resolution_mutualdefense_renegade_containment"
		}
	}

	allow = {
	}

	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_normal
	}
}

resolution_divinity_a_defined_purpose = {
	icon = "GFX_resolution_robots_bad"

	potential = {
		has_federations_dlc = yes
	}

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t5
		}
	}
	target = no
	level = 5

	modifier = {
		resolution_divinity_comfort_the_fallen = 1
		resolution_divinity_tithe_on_the_soulless = 1
		resolution_divinity_right_to_work_fixed = 1
		resolution_divinity_silence_the_soulless = 1
		resolution_divinity_a_defined_purpose = 1
	}

	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = resolution_divinity_a_defined_purpose_effect
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed_divinity days = @resolution_flag_timer }
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = resolution_passed_diplomatic_weight
				days = 2200
			}
			every_playable_country = {
				limit = {
					is_galactic_community_member = yes
					in_breach_of = resolution_divinity_a_defined_purpose
				}
				country_event = { id = federations.10340 }
			}
		}
	}

	fail_effects = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_failed_divinity days = @resolution_flag_timer }
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = resolution_failed_diplomatic_weight
				days = 2200
			}
		}
	}

	allow = {
		is_active_resolution = "resolution_divinity_silence_the_soulless"
	}

	breach = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				is_machine_empire = no
				has_policy_flag = ai_full_rights
			}
			AND = {
				is_machine_empire = yes
				NOT = { has_valid_civic = civic_machine_servitor }
			}
		}

	}

	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_disliked

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			has_ai_personality_behaviour = robot_exploiter
			NOT = { has_valid_civic = civic_machine_servitor }
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			has_ai_personality_behaviour = robot_liberator
			NOT = { has_valid_civic = civic_machine_servitor }
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			is_gestalt = yes
			NOT = { has_valid_civic = civic_machine_servitor }
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_synthetic_empire = yes
			NOT = { has_valid_civic = civic_machine_servitor }
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			NOR = {
				has_ai_personality_behaviour = robot_exploiter
				has_ai_personality_behaviour = robot_liberator
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			is_spiritualist = yes
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 100
			has_valid_civic = civic_machine_servitor
		}
	}
}

		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_failed_divinity days = @resolution_flag_timer }
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = resolution_failed_diplomatic_weight
				days = 2200
			}
		}
	}

	allow = {
		is_active_resolution = "resolution_divinity_a_defined_purpose"
	}

	breach = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				is_machine_empire = no
				has_policy_flag = ai_servitude
			}
			AND = {
				is_machine_empire = no
				has_policy_flag = ai_full_rights
			}
			AND = {
				is_machine_empire = yes
				NOT = { has_valid_civic = civic_machine_servitor }
			}
		}

	}

	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_hated

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			has_ai_personality_behaviour = robot_exploiter
			NOT = { has_valid_civic = civic_machine_servitor }
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			has_ai_personality_behaviour = robot_liberator
			NOT = { has_valid_civic = civic_machine_servitor }
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			is_machine_empire = yes
			NOT = { has_valid_civic = civic_machine_servitor }
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_synthetic_empire = yes
			NOT = { has_valid_civic = civic_machine_servitor }
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			NOR = {
				has_ai_personality_behaviour = robot_exploiter
				has_ai_personality_behaviour = robot_liberator
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 2.5
			is_spiritualist = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_spiritualist = no
			NOT = { has_valid_civic = civic_machine_servitor }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 100
			has_valid_civic = civic_machine_servitor
		}
	}
}

# GALACTIC REFORMS

resolution_galacticreforms_abolish_council = {
	icon = "GFX_resolution_council_veto"

	potential = {
		has_federations_dlc = yes
	}

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t5
		}
	}
	target = no

	modifier = {
	}

	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = resolution_galacticreforms_abolish_council_tooltip
		hidden_effect = {
			set_council_size = 0
			remove_global_flag = galactic_council_formed
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed_general days = @resolution_flag_timer }
		}
	}

	fail_effects = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_failed_general days = @resolution_flag_timer }
		}
	}

	potential = {
		has_global_flag = galactic_council_formed
	}

	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_hated

		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_part_of_galactic_council = yes
			NOT = { has_ai_personality = democratic_crusaders }
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			is_part_of_galactic_council = no
			has_ai_personality = democratic_crusaders
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_subject = yes
			overlord = {
				opinion_level = { who = prev level >= neutral }
				is_part_of_galactic_council = yes
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			OR = {
				has_civic = civic_diplomatic_corps
				has_civic = civic_public_relations_specialists
				has_civic = civic_hive_empath
				has_civic = civic_machine_servitor
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.1
			is_egalitarian = yes
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			OR = {
				is_gestalt = yes
				is_xenophobe = yes
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			is_xenophile = yes
		}
	}
}

resolution_galacticreforms_form_council = {
	icon = "GFX_resolution_create_council"

	potential = {
		has_federations_dlc = yes
		NOT = { has_global_flag = galactic_council_formed }
	}

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t1
		}
	}
	target = no

	modifier = {
	}

	allow = {
		is_years_since_community_formation >= 20
	}

	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = resolution_galacticreforms_form_council_tooltip
		hidden_effect = {
			set_council_size = 3
			set_council_veto = no
			remove_global_flag = resolution_council_denouncement_abolished
			set_global_flag = galactic_council_formed
			set_global_flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed

			set_global_flag = resolution_with_breach_effect_passed # council denouncement

			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed_general days = @resolution_flag_timer }
		}
	}

	fail_effects = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_failed_general days = @resolution_flag_timer }
		}
	}

	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_loved

		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			OR = {
				has_civic = civic_diplomatic_corps
				has_civic = civic_public_relations_specialists
				has_civic = civic_hive_empath
				has_civic = civic_machine_servitor
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			OR = {
				galactic_community_rank <= 3
				AND = {
					is_subject = yes
					overlord = {
						opinion_level = { who = prev level >= neutral }
						galactic_community_rank <= 3
					}
				}
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.1
			is_authoritarian = yes
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			OR = {
				is_gestalt = yes
				is_xenophobe = yes
				is_egalitarian = yes
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			galactic_community_rank > 5
			NAND = {
				is_subject = yes
				overlord = {
					opinion_level = { who = prev level >= neutral }
					galactic_community_rank <= 3
				}
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			OR = {
				has_ai_personality = democratic_crusaders
				has_valid_civic = civic_shared_burden
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.1
			is_xenophile = yes
		}
	}
}

			set_council_veto = no
			remove_global_flag = galactic_council_veto
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed_general days = @resolution_flag_timer }
		}
	}

	fail_effects = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_failed_general days = @resolution_flag_timer }
		}
	}

	potential = {
		has_global_flag = galactic_council_formed
		has_global_flag = galactic_council_veto
	}

	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_disliked

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			OR = {
				has_civic = civic_diplomatic_corps
				has_civic = civic_public_relations_specialists
				has_civic = civic_hive_empath
				has_civic = civic_machine_servitor
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			is_authoritarian = yes
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			OR = {
				is_part_of_galactic_council = yes
				AND = {
					is_subject = yes
					overlord = {
						opinion_level = { who = prev level >= neutral }
						is_part_of_galactic_council = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

resolution_galacticreforms_disable_council_denouncement = {
	icon = "GFX_resolution_council_veto"

	potential = {
		has_federations_dlc = yes
	}

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t4
		}
	}
	target = no

	modifier = {
	}

	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = resolution_galacticreforms_disable_council_denouncement_tooltip
		hidden_effect = {
			set_global_flag = resolution_council_denouncement_abolished
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed_general days = @resolution_flag_timer }
		}
	}

	fail_effects = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_failed_general days = @resolution_flag_timer }
		}
	}

	potential = {
		has_global_flag = galactic_council_formed
		NOT = { has_global_flag = resolution_council_denouncement_abolished }
	}

	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_disliked

		modifier = {
			factor = 2.5
			has_modifier = resolution_denounced
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			OR = {
				has_civic = civic_diplomatic_corps
				has_civic = civic_public_relations_specialists
				has_civic = civic_hive_empath
				has_civic = civic_machine_servitor
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			is_authoritarian = yes
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			OR = {
				is_part_of_galactic_council = yes
				AND = {
					is_subject = yes
					overlord = {
						opinion_level = { who = prev level >= neutral }
						is_part_of_galactic_council = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			any_relation = {
				is_in_federation_with = prev

				OR = {
					is_in_breach_of_any = yes
					has_modifier = resolution_denounced
				}
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			any_relation = {
				is_rival = prev

				OR = {
					is_in_breach_of_any = yes
					has_modifier = resolution_denounced
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

resolution_sanctions_tech_repeal_1 = {
	icon = "GFX_repeal_blue"

	resources = {

		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_denounce
		}
	}
	target = no

	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = resolution_sanctions_tech_repeal_1_effect_success
	}

	potential = {
		is_active_resolution = "resolution_sanctions_tech_1"
	}

	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_unpopular

		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_in_breach_of_any = yes
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			is_in_breach_of_any = no
			is_materialist = yes
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			any_relation = {
				is_in_federation_with = prev

				OR = {
					is_in_breach_of_any = yes
					has_modifier = resolution_denounced
				}
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			any_relation = {
				is_rival = prev

				OR = {
					is_in_breach_of_any = yes
					has_modifier = resolution_denounced
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

				is_active_resolution = "resolution_sanctions_tech_1"
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_sanctions_tech_2"
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_sanctions_tech_3"
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_sanctions_tech_4"
			}
		}
	}

	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_normal

		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_in_breach_of_any = yes
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			is_in_breach_of_any = no
			is_materialist = yes
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			any_relation = {
				is_in_federation_with = prev

				OR = {
					is_in_breach_of_any = yes
					has_modifier = resolution_denounced
				}
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			any_relation = {
				is_rival = prev

				OR = {
					is_in_breach_of_any = yes
					has_modifier = resolution_denounced
				}
			}
		}
	}

			}
		}

		}
	}

		is_part_of_galactic_council = yes
	}

		weight = @resolution_weight_normal

		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_in_breach_of_any = yes

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			is_in_breach_of_any = no
			is_megacorp = yes
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			any_relation = {
				is_in_federation_with = prev

				OR = {
					is_in_breach_of_any = yes
					has_modifier = resolution_denounced
				}
			}
		}

resolution_repeal_tiyanki_pest_control = {
	icon = "GFX_repeal_red"

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_denounce
		}
	}

	target = no

	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = resolution_repeal_tiyanki_pest_control_effect_success
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed_ecology_repeal days = @resolution_flag_timer }
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = resolution_passed_diplomatic_weight
				days = 2200
			}
		}
	}

	fail_effects = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_failed_ecology_repeal days = @resolution_flag_timer }
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = resolution_failed_diplomatic_weight
				days = 2200
			}
		}
	}

	potential = {
		is_active_resolution = "resolution_tiyanki_pest_control"
	}

	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_disliked

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			is_xenophile = yes
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			is_pacifist = yes
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			is_militarist = yes
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			OR = {
				has_valid_civic = civic_environmentalist
				has_valid_civic = civic_hive_empath
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_xenophobe = yes
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 10
			in_breach_of = resolution_tiyanki_pest_control
		}
	}
}

resolution_amoeba_conservation_act = {
	icon = "GFX_resolution_tiyanki_preservation"

	potential = {
		has_federations_dlc = yes
		has_modifier = pacified_amoebas
	}

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_denounce
		}
	}
	target = no

	modifier = {
	}

	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = resolution_amoeba_conservation_act_tooltip
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					is_galactic_community_member = yes
					NOT = { has_modifier = pacified_amoebas }
				}
				country_event = { id = galactic_features.505 }
			}
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed_general days = @resolution_flag_timer }
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = resolution_passed_diplomatic_weight
				days = 2200
			}
		}
	}

	fail_effects = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_failed_general days = @resolution_flag_timer }
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = resolution_failed_diplomatic_weight
				days = 2200
			}
		}
	}

	potential = {
	}

	allow = {
		is_active_resolution = resolution_tiyanki_conservation_act
	}

	breach = {
		NOT = { has_modifier = pacified_amoebas }
	}

	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_disliked

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			is_xenophile = yes
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			is_pacifist = yes
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			is_militarist = yes
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			OR = {
				has_valid_civic = civic_environmentalist
				has_valid_civic = civic_hive_empath
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_xenophobe = yes
		}
	}
}

		}
	}

	}

		custom_tooltip = resolution_galactic_market_ban_sentient_organic_slave_trade_effect_success
		hidden_effect = {

			}
		}
	}

	fail_effects = {

				modifier = resolution_failed_diplomatic_weight
				days = 2200
			}
		}
	}

	potential = {
		NOT = {
			is_active_resolution = "resolution_galactic_market_ban_sentient_organic_slave_trade"
			has_global_flag = organic_slave_trade_banned_flag
		}
	}

	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_disliked

			factor = 1.5

		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5

		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_xenophobe = yes
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_authoritarian = yes
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_slaver = yes
		}
	}
}

resolution_galactic_market_relocate = {
	icon = "GFX_resolution_relocate_galactic_market"

	potential = {
		has_federations_dlc = yes
	}

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t1
		}
	}
	target = no

	allow = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			fail_text = "resolution_galactic_market_relocate_trigger_fail"
			NOT = {
				has_global_flag = "resolution_galactic_market_relocated_recently"
			}
		}
	}

	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = resolution_galactic_market_relocate_effect_success
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = galcom.64 }

			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed_general days = @resolution_flag_timer }

			add_modifier = {
				modifier = resolution_passed_diplomatic_weight
				days = 2200
			}

			set_timed_global_flag = { flag = resolution_galactic_market_relocated_recently days = 18000 }
		}
	}

	fail_effects = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_failed_general days = @resolution_flag_timer }
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = resolution_failed_diplomatic_weight
				days = 2200
			}
		}
	}

	modifier = {
	}

	potential = {
		has_global_flag = galactic_market_founded
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = ongoing_market_relocation_nomination
		}
		NOT = { has_modifier = galactic_market_founder }
		is_gestalt = no
		is_homicidal = no
	}

	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_disliked

		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			has_modifier = galactic_market_founder
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			any_federation_ally = {
				has_modifier = galactic_market_founder
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_gestalt = no
			has_resource = { type = influence amount < 400 }
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			is_gestalt = no
			has_resource = { type = influence amount > 700 }
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			has_authority = auth_corporate
			NOT = { has_modifier = galactic_market_founder }
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			OR = {
				has_ai_personality = peaceful_traders
				has_ai_personality = ruthless_capitalists
			}
			NOT = { has_modifier = galactic_market_founder }
		}
	}
}

#1: Authoritarian
resolution_stratification_repeal_1 = {
	icon = "GFX_repeal_blue"

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t1
		}
	}
	target = no

	potential = {
		is_active_resolution = "resolution_enlightened_despotism"
	}

	allow = {}

	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_unpopular

		modifier = {
			factor = 3
			is_egalitarian = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			NOT = {
				has_ai_personality_behaviour = slaver
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_authoritarian = yes
		}
	}
}

resolution_enlightened_despotism = {
	icon = "GFX_sanctions_purple"

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t1
		}
	}
	target = no
	level = 1

	modifier = {
		resolution_enlightened_despotism = 1
	}

	effect = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_global_flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed
		}
	}
	allow = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			fail_text = "resolution_already_active"
			NOR = {		
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_enlightened_despotism"
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_a_proper_place"
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_natural_hierarchy"
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_superior_deference"
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_a_whiff_of_grapeshot"
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_let_them_eat_cake"
			}
		}
	}

	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_loved

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_egalitarian = yes
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_authoritarian = yes
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			OR = {
				has_valid_civic = civic_slaver_guilds
				has_valid_civic = civic_indentured_assets
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			is_gestalt = yes #This resolution does nothing to gestalts
		}
	}
}

resolution_natural_hierarchy = {
	icon = "GFX_repeal_blue"

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t3
		}
	}
	target = no
	level = 3

	modifier = {
		resolution_enlightened_despotism = 1
		resolution_a_proper_place = 1
		resolution_natural_hierarchy = 1
	}

	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = resolution_natural_hierarchy_effect
		hidden_effect = {
			set_global_flag = resolution_with_breach_effect_passed
		}
	}

	allow = {
		is_active_resolution = "resolution_a_proper_place"
	}

	breach = {
		AND = {
			is_gestalt = no
			any_owned_species = {
				is_sapient = yes
				OR = {
					has_living_standard = { type = living_standard_shared_burden country = prev }
					has_living_standard = { type = living_standard_utopian country = prev }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_normal

		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			has_valid_civic = civic_shared_burden
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			is_egalitarian = yes
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_authoritarian = yes
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 3 #Great for slavers
			OR = {
				has_valid_civic = civic_slaver_guilds
				has_valid_civic = civic_indentured_assets
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			is_gestalt = yes #This resolution does nothing to gestalts
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.6 #This pisses off specialists
			is_authoritarian = no
		}
	}
}

resolution_stratification_repeal_4 = {
	icon = "GFX_repeal_blue"

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t4
		}
	}
	target = no

	effect = {
		hidden_effect = {
			pass_resolution = "resolution_natural_hierarchy"
		}
	}

	potential = {
		is_active_resolution = "resolution_superior_deference"
	}

	modifier = {
		resolution_enlightened_despotism = 1
		resolution_a_proper_place = 1
		resolution_natural_hierarchy = 1
	}

	allow = {}

	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_normal

		modifier = {
			factor = 5
			is_egalitarian = yes
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 10
			has_valid_civic = civic_shared_burden
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.4
			is_authoritarian = yes
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			has_valid_civic = civic_slaver_guilds
			has_valid_civic = civic_indentured_assets
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 3
			NOT = {
				has_ai_personality_behaviour = slaver
			}
		}
	}
}

resolution_superior_deference = {
	icon = "GFX_repeal_blue"

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t4
		}
	}
	target = no
	level = 4

	modifier = {
		resolution_enlightened_despotism = 1
		resolution_a_proper_place = 1
		resolution_natural_hierarchy = 1
		resolution_superior_deference = 1
	}

	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = resolution_superior_deference_effect
		hidden_effect = {
			set_global_flag = resolution_with_breach_effect_passed
		}
	}
	allow = {
		is_active_resolution = "resolution_natural_hierarchy"
	}

	breach = {
		AND = {
			is_gestalt = no
			any_owned_species = {
				is_sapient = yes
				OR = {
					has_living_standard = { type = living_standard_shared_burden country = prev }
					has_living_standard = { type = living_standard_utopian country = prev }
					has_living_standard = { type = living_standard_good country = prev }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_normal

		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			has_valid_civic = civic_shared_burden
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.1
			is_egalitarian = yes
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_authoritarian = yes
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 4 #Great for slavers
			OR = {
				has_valid_civic = civic_slaver_guilds
				has_valid_civic = civic_indentured_assets
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			is_gestalt = yes #This resolution does nothing to gestalts
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.4 #This pisses off specialists... and makes them BAD
			is_authoritarian = no
		}
	}
}

resolution_intercultural_exchange = {
	icon = "GFX_sanctions_purple"

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t1
		}
	}
	target = no
	level = 1

	modifier = {
		resolution_intercultural_exchange = 1
	}

	effect = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_global_flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed
			#set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed_ecology days = @resolution_flag_timer }
		}
	}

	fail_effects = {
		hidden_effect = {
			#set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_failed_ecology days = @resolution_flag_timer }
		}
	}

	allow = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			fail_text = "resolution_already_active"
			NOR = {		
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_intercultural_exchange"
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_strength_in_diversity"
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_charter_of_sentient_rights"
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_stellar_diplomatic_forums"
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_prime_directive"
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_galactic_cooperation_initiative"
			}
		}
	}

	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_loved #Nothing but benefits for non-xenophobes

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_xenophobe = yes #Even normal xenophobes don't HATE it
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.2
			has_valid_civic = civic_inwards_perfection #Inward perfectionists, on the other hand
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 3
			is_xenophile = yes #Duh
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			OR = {
				has_valid_civic = civic_merchant_guilds
				is_megacorp = yes #Trade-heavy empires like + trade value
				has_ai_personality_behaviour = multispecies 
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_pacifist = yes #Pacifists prefer talking to fighting, and this helps talking
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			is_gestalt = yes #This resolution does less for gestalts, but not nothing
		}
	}
}

resolution_charter_of_sentient_rights = {
	icon = "GFX_repeal_blue"

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t3
		}
	}
	target = no
	level = 3

	modifier = {
		resolution_intercultural_exchange = 1
		resolution_strength_in_diversity = 1
		resolution_charter_of_sentient_rights = 1
	}

	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = resolution_charter_of_sentient_rights_effect
		hidden_effect = {
			set_global_flag = resolution_with_breach_effect_passed
			#set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed_rulesofwar days = @resolution_flag_timer }

			#every_playable_country = {
			#	limit = {
			#		is_galactic_community_member = yes
			#		has_policy_flag = purge_allowed
			#	}
			#	country_event = { id = federations.10300 }
			#}
		}
	}

	fail_effects = {
		hidden_effect = {
			#set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_failed_rulesofwar days = @resolution_flag_timer }
		}
	}

	allow = {
		is_active_resolution = "resolution_strength_in_diversity"
	}

	breach = {
		OR = { #Everyone has a right to full citizenship
			#None of this "residence" crap
			#And don't get me started on purging
			any_owned_species = {
				is_sapient = yes
				OR = {
					has_citizenship_type = { type = citizenship_slavery country = prev }
					has_citizenship_type = { type = citizenship_limited country = prev }
				}
			}
			AND = {
				is_gestalt = no #For gestalts, kicking sentients out is the BEST option...
				has_policy_flag = purge_displacement_only
			}
			has_policy_flag = purge_allowed
			
		}
	}
	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_liked #Mostly benefits for non-xenophobes/militarists after early game

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.3
			is_xenophobe = yes 
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 10
			has_federation = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.1
			has_valid_civic = civic_inwards_perfection #Inward perfectionists, on the other hand
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 5
			is_xenophile = yes #Duh
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			OR = {
				has_valid_civic = civic_merchant_guilds
				is_megacorp = yes #Trade-heavy empires like + trade value
				has_ai_personality_behaviour = multispecies 
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 3
			is_pacifist = yes #Pacifists prefer talking to fighting, and this helps talking, and hurts fighting
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.4

resolution_stellar_diplomatic_forums = {
	icon = "GFX_repeal_blue"

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t4
		}
	}
	target = no
	level = 4

	modifier = {
		resolution_intercultural_exchange = 1
		resolution_strength_in_diversity = 1
		resolution_charter_of_sentient_rights = 1
		resolution_stellar_diplomatic_forums = 1
	}

	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = resolution_stellar_diplomatic_forums_effect
		hidden_effect = {
			set_global_flag = resolution_with_breach_effect_passed
			#set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed_rulesofwar days = @resolution_flag_timer }

			#every_playable_country = {
			#	limit = {
			#		is_galactic_community_member = yes
			#		has_policy_flag = purge_allowed
			#	}
			#	country_event = { id = federations.10300 }
			#}
		}
	}

	fail_effects = {
		hidden_effect = {
			#set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_failed_rulesofwar days = @resolution_flag_timer }
		}
	}

	allow = {
		is_active_resolution = "resolution_charter_of_sentient_rights"
	}

	breach = {
		OR = { #Everyone has a right to full citizenship
			#None of this "residence" crap
			#And don't get me started on purging
			any_owned_species = {
				is_sapient = yes
				OR = {
					has_citizenship_type = { type = citizenship_slavery country = prev }
					has_citizenship_type = { type = citizenship_limited country = prev }
				}
			}
			AND = {
				is_gestalt = no #For gestalts, kicking sentients out is the BEST option...
				has_policy_flag = purge_displacement_only
			}
			has_policy_flag = purge_allowed
			has_policy_flag = diplo_stance_belligerent
			has_policy_flag = diplo_stance_supremacist
		}
	}
	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_liked #Mostly benefits for non-xenophobes/militarists after early game

		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_xenophobe = yes 
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 10
			has_federation = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			has_valid_civic = civic_inwards_perfection #Inward perfectionists, on the other hand
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 5
			is_xenophile = yes #Duh
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			OR = {
				has_valid_civic = civic_merchant_guilds
				is_megacorp = yes #Trade-heavy empires like + trade value
				has_ai_personality_behaviour = multispecies 
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 3
			is_pacifist = yes #Pacifists prefer talking to fighting, and this helps talking, and hurts fighting
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.3
			is_gestalt = yes #Don't vote for something that makes you treat other sentients as equals
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.2
			is_militarist = yes #Increased claim cost is bad
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			OR = {
				has_policy_flag = diplo_stance_expansionist
				has_policy_flag = diplo_stance_belligerent
				has_policy_flag = diplo_stance_supremacist
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			in_breach_of = resolution_stellar_diplomatic_forums
		}
	}
}

resolution_prime_directive = {
	icon = "GFX_repeal_blue"

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t5
		}
	}
	target = no
	level = 5

	modifier = {
		resolution_intercultural_exchange = 1
		resolution_strength_in_diversity = 1
		resolution_charter_of_sentient_rights = 1
		resolution_stellar_diplomatic_forums = 1
		resolution_prime_directive = 1
	}

	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = resolution_prime_directive_effect
		hidden_effect = {
			set_global_flag = resolution_with_breach_effect_passed
			#set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed_rulesofwar days = @resolution_flag_timer }

			#every_playable_country = {
			#	limit = {
			#		is_galactic_community_member = yes
			#		has_policy_flag = purge_allowed
			#	}
			#	country_event = { id = federations.10300 }

		}

		hidden_effect = {
			#set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_failed_rulesofwar days = @resolution_flag_timer }
		}
	}

	allow = {
		is_active_resolution = "resolution_stellar_diplomatic_forums"
	}

	breach = {
		OR = { #Everyone has a right to full citizenship
			#None of this "residence" crap
			#And don't get me started on purging
			any_owned_species = {
				is_sapient = yes
				OR = {
					has_citizenship_type = { type = citizenship_slavery country = prev }
					has_citizenship_type = { type = citizenship_limited country = prev }
				}
			}
			AND = {
				is_gestalt = no #For gestalts, kicking sentients out is the BEST option...
				has_policy_flag = purge_displacement_only
			}
			has_policy_flag = purge_allowed
			has_policy_flag = diplo_stance_belligerent
			has_policy_flag = diplo_stance_supremacist
			#Primitives are people too!
			has_policy_flag = interference_active
			has_policy_flag = interference_full
		}
	}
	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_normal #Lots of restrictions

		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_xenophobe = yes 
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 10
			has_federation = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			has_valid_civic = civic_inwards_perfection
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 6
			is_xenophile = yes #Duh
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			OR = {
				has_valid_civic = civic_merchant_guilds
				is_megacorp = yes #Trade-heavy empires like + trade value
				has_ai_personality_behaviour = multispecies 
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 4
			is_pacifist = yes #Pacifists prefer talking to fighting, and this helps talking, and hurts fighting
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.1
			is_gestalt = yes #Don't vote for something that makes you treat other sentients as equals
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.1
			is_militarist = yes #Increased claim cost is bad
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			OR = {
				has_policy_flag = diplo_stance_expansionist
				has_policy_flag = diplo_stance_belligerent
				has_policy_flag = diplo_stance_supremacist
				has_policy_flag = diplo_stance_isolationist
			}
		}
		modifier = {

			in_breach_of = resolution_prime_directive

			factor = 0.8

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			is_gestalt = yes #This resolution does less for gestalts, but not nothing
		}

		}
	}

resolution_national_purity = {
	icon = "GFX_repeal_blue"

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t4
		}
	}
	target = no
	level = 4

	modifier = {
		resolution_guarded_sovereignty = 1
		resolution_homogenous_state = 1
		resolution_justified_suspicion = 1
		resolution_national_purity = 1
	}

	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = resolution_national_purity_effect
		hidden_effect = {
			set_global_flag = resolution_with_breach_effect_passed
		}
	}

	allow = {
		is_active_resolution = "resolution_justified_suspicion"
	}

	breach = {
		OR = {
			has_policy_flag = refugees_allowed
			has_diplo_migration_treaty = yes
			has_policy_flag = diplo_stance_cooperative
			#No citizen rights for you!
			AND = {
				is_gestalt = no #Hives shouldn't get f***ed by this
				any_owned_species = {
					NOT = {is_same_species = prev}
					is_sapient = yes
					is_robotic = no
					OR = {
						has_citizenship_type = { type = citizenship_full country = prev }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_hated 

		modifier = {
			factor = 4
			is_xenophobe = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 4
			has_valid_civic = civic_inwards_perfection 
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.2
			OR = {
				has_valid_civic = civic_merchant_guilds
				is_megacorp = yes #Trade-heavy empires like + trade value
				has_ai_personality_behaviour = multispecies 
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			is_pacifist = yes #Pacifists prefer talking to fighting, and this hurts talking
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			is_gestalt = yes #This resolution does less for gestalts, but not nothing
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			in_breach_of = resolution_national_purity
		}
	}
}
